***леность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:леность.html>ле́ность</a> (31854)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěnostь</i>, based off of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěnъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lazy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лѣнꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lěnyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be"><a href = vnd.unilang:лян.html>ляны́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljaný</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">лен</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">len</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">ли̏jен</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">líný</i>, etc. Synchronically composed as if from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*лено́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*lenój</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lazy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based off of a no-longer existing adjectival form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лень.html>лень</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lenʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">laziness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, replaced in modern Russian with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ленивый.html>лени́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lenívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (but dialectal <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">лено́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lenój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is still found).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:леность.html>ле́ность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lénostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:леность.html>ле́ности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:леность.html>ле́ности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:леность.html>ле́ностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>laziness, indolence, idleness, sloth</li></ol>

***лента.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лента.html>ле́нта</a> (2776)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Linte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ribbon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lint</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ribbon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лента.html>ле́нта</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lénta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лента.html>ле́нты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лента.html>ле́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лента.html>ле́нт</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ribbon, band</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tape
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клейкий.html>кле́йкая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лента.html>ле́нта</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kléjkaja <b>lénta</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">duct tape</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">weaponry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> belt</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">culture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> film, movie</li></ol>

***лентяй.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лентяй.html>лентя́й</a> (16104)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лентяй.html>лентя́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lentjáj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лентяй.html>лентя́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лентяй.html>лентя́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лентяй.html>лентя́ев</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">лентя́йка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lazybones, loafer, idler, slacker, sluggard</li></ol>

<p><b>лен<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тя́й</b>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лепетать.html>лепета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lepetátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залепетать.html>залепета́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролепетать.html>пролепета́ть</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лепешка.html>лепёшка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lepjóška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лепешка.html>лепёшки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лепешка.html>лепёшки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лепешка.html>лепёшек</a></b>)

<ol><li>flatbread, flat cake, cookie

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коровий.html>коро́вья</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лепешка.html>лепёшка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">koróvʹja <b>lepjóška</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">cow's dropping</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>tablet, lozenge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мятный.html>мя́тная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лепешка.html>лепёшка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mjátnaja <b>lepjóška</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mint <b>lozenge</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***лепить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лепить.html>лепи́ть</a> (8879)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěpiti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лепить.html>лепи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lepítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вылепить.html>вы́лепить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слепить.html>слепи́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:налепить.html>налепи́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залепить.html>залепи́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влепить.html>влепи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to model, to sculpt, to fashion, to shape
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вылепить.html>вы́лепить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výlepitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to build, to make (cells, a nest, etc.)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слепить.html>слепи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">slepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stick on
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:налепить.html>налепи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nalepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slap, to smack
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:залепить.html>залепи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zalepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:влепить.html>влепи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vlepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to babble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лепить.html>лепи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вздор.html>вздор</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lepítʹ</b> vzdor</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to talk nonsense</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лепиться.html>лепи́ться</a> (20179)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лепить.html>лепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

***лес.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a> (280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лѣсъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lěsŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěsъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">les</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>ле́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>леса́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лесо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Russian-forest"> forest, woods
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>леса́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lesá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">woodland, forests</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:девственный.html>де́вственный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dévstvennyj <b>les</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">virgin forest, primeval forest</span></div></dd>
<dd><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заповедный.html>запове́дный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zapovédnyj les</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> means:
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заповедник.html>запове́дник</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zapovédnik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">protection forest</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тайный.html>та́йный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:священный.html>свяще́нный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:божий.html>бо́жий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tájnyj <b>les</b>, svjaščénnyj <b>les</b>, bóžij <b>les</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sacred forest, a forest that nobody may enter</span></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корабельный.html>корабе́льный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">korabélʹnyj <b>les</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">ship timber</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лиственный.html>ли́ственный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lístvennyj <b>les</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">leaf-bearing forest</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешанный.html>сме́шанный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sméšannyj <b>les</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mixed forest</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тропический.html>тропи́ческий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tropíčeskij <b>les</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">rainforest</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хвойный.html>хво́йный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xvójnyj <b>les</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">coniferous forest</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чаща.html>ча́ща</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>леса</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čášča lesa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">thicket, the depths of forest</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шум.html>шум</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>леса</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">šum lesa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">murmur of the forest</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лесу́</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak v lesú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at sea, lost, disoriented</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрова.html>дрова́</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kto v <b>les</b>, kto po drová</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(to be) at sixes and sevens</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">some go to the forest, some go for firewood</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубить.html>ру́бят</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:щепка.html>ще́пки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лететь.html>летя́т</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>les</b> rúbjat — ščépki letját</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you can’t make an omelette without breaking eggs</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">when cutting trees, chips fly</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> тёмный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">(dlja nevó) éto tjómnyj <b>les</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it is all Greek (to him), (he is) completely in the dark about it</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">this is the dark forest for him</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дремучий.html>дрему́чий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">(dlja nevó) éto dremúčij <b>les</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it is all Greek (to him), (he is) completely in the dark about it</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">this is the dark forest for him</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лесу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́ди</a> лесеют, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́дях</a> людеют</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v lesú ljúdi lesejut, a v ljúdjax ljudejut</i> ― <small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">in the forest people become wild, and become people among people</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чей.html>чей</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пень.html>пень</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čej <b>les</b>, tovó i penʹ</i> ― <small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">the man who owns a forest, also owns a stump</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>Бог</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>ле́су</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> сравня́л</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Box i <b>lésu</b> ne sravnjál</i> ― <span class="e-translation">people are not equal</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">God doesn’t even make the forest equal</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(only <i>singular</i>) lumber, timber
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>ле́с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плот.html>плота́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lés</b> v plotáx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">timber float</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>ле́с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>корню́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lés</b> na kornjú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">standing timber</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(only <i>plural</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>леса́</a> scaffolding, scaffold trestle, falsework
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>леса́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lesá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">scaffolding, scaffold trestle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> much, many, a lot of <i>smth.</i> (especially high, eminent)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>les</b> ruk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a forest of hands <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in school if nobody wants to answer the teacher’s question, it's used sarcastically, when nobody actually raises a hand, there is no "forest of hands", not a single "tree", i.e. hand</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мачта.html>ма́чт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>les</b> mačt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a large number of ships</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:штык.html>штыко́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>les</b> štykóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">forest of bayonets</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесник.html>лесни́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lesník</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span>, <span class="ann-pos">adjectival suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесничий.html>лесни́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lesníčij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесничий.html>лесни́чего</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесничий.html>лесни́чие</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесничий.html>лесни́чих</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>woodsman, forest ranger, chief forester</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>This noun does <b>not</b> decline the same way as the relational adjective, and is derived from an etymologically different suffix.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесник.html>лесни́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lesník</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span>, <span class="ann-pos">possessive suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">les</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воз.html>воз</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, combining form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to convey</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:леспромхоз.html>леспромхо́з</a> (17997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">лесопромы́шленное <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйство.html>хозя́йство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lesopromýšlennoje xozjájstvo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">logging industry enterprise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесной.html>лесно́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:промышленный.html>промы́шленное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйство.html>хозя́йство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lesnóje promýšlennoje xozjájstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***лестница.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лестница.html>ле́стница</a> (920)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лѣстница</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lěstnica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, derived from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lěstva</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lězti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to climb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-tv-</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лезть.html>лезть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">leztʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ница</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лестница.html>ле́стница</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">léstnica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лестница.html>ле́стницы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лестница.html>ле́стницы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лестница.html>ле́стниц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stair, staircase
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лестница.html>ле́стнице</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nádo býlo idtí po <b>léstnice</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You should have taken <b>the stairs</b>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбегать.html>сбега́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лестница.html>ле́стницы</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbegátʹ s <b>léstnicy</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run down<b>stairs</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>ladder, step</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесть.html>лесть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>complimentary</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ле́ст<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>лестне́е.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-лест-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
